<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:втыкать.html>втыка́ть</a> (19794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тыкать.html>ты́кать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">týkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втыкать.html>втыка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vtykátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воткнуть.html>воткну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(in, into)</i>, to drive <i>(in, into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втыкать.html>втыка́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>кол</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>зе́млю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtykátʹ</b> kol v zémlju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive a stake into the ground</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***втягивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a> (9279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">втяг-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vtjag-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vtjágivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуть.html>втяну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pull <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in, into, on, up</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to draw <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in, into, on, up</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to take in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здух</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjágivatʹ</b> vózdux</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to draw/breathe/take in air</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жидкость.html>жи́дкость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjágivatʹ</b> žídkostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take in (suck up; absorb) liquid</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:коготь.html>ко́гти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjágivatʹ</b> kógti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to draw in its claws</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёки</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:живот.html>живо́т</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjágivatʹ</b> ščóki (živót)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to suck/pull in one's cheeks (stomach)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to draw <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">into</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to get involved <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***втягиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:втягиваться.html>втя́гиваться</a> (22477)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vtjágivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втягиваться.html>втя́гиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vtjágivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуться.html>втяну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sag, to fall in</li>
<li>to get used, to get accustomed <i>(to)</i>, to feel at home <i>(with)</i>, to take <i>(to)</i>, to develop a liking <i>(for)</i>, to begin to enjoy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втягиваться.html>втя́гиваться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пьянство.html>пья́нство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjágivatʹsja</b> v pʹjánstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take to drinking</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get mixed up <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втягиваться.html>втя́гиваться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязный.html>гря́зную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тику</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjágivatʹsja</b> v grjáznuju polítiku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get mixed up in dirty politics</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vtjágivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:втянуть.html>втяну́ть</a> (6751)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуть.html>втяну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vtjanútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pull <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in, into, on, up</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to draw <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in, into, on, up</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to take in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуть.html>втяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здух</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjanútʹ</b> vózdux</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to draw/breathe/take in air</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуть.html>втяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жидкость.html>жи́дкость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjanútʹ</b> žídkostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take in (suck up; absorb) liquid</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуть.html>втяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:коготь.html>ко́гти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjanútʹ</b> kógti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to draw in its claws</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуть.html>втяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёки</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:живот.html>живо́т</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjanútʹ</b> ščóki (živót)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to suck/pull in one's cheeks (stomach)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to draw <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">into</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to get involved <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:втянуться.html>втяну́ться</a> (15418)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуть.html>втяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vtjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуться.html>втяну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vtjanútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втягиваться.html>втя́гиваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sag, to fall in</li>
<li>to get used, to get accustomed <i>(to)</i>, to feel at home <i>(with)</i>, to take <i>(to)</i>, to develop a liking <i>(for)</i>, to begin to enjoy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуться.html>втяну́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пьянство.html>пья́нство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjanútʹsja</b> v pʹjánstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take to drinking</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get mixed up <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуться.html>втяну́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязный.html>гря́зную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тику</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjanútʹsja</b> v grjáznuju polítiku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get mixed up in dirty politics</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуть.html>втяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vtjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***входить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:входить.html>входи́ть</a> (936)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:входить.html>входи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:войти.html>войти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to enter, to go in(to) (by foot), to get in(to)</li>
<li>to penetrate into</li>
<li>to be a part of</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вход.html>вход</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vxod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:входной.html>входно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vxodnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> entrance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:входной.html>входна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vxodnája</b> dverʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>entrance</b> door</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:входной.html>входно́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vxodnój</b> bilét</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>entrance</b> ticket/card; ticket of admittance</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:входной.html>входна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:плат.html>пла́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vxodnája</b> pláta</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>entrance</b> fee</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:входной.html>входно́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>отве́рстие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vxodnóje</b> otvérstije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">inlet</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>entrance</b> passage</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***вцепиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вцепиться.html>вцепи́ться</a> (3857)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-цепи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-cepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вцепиться.html>вцепи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vcepítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вцепляться.html>вцепля́ться</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to seize, to grasp, to clutch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:злобный.html>зло́бно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вцепиться.html>вцепи́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná zlóbno <b>vcepílasʹ</b> jemú v vólosy.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She viciously seized him by the hair.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cling <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a sticky object</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to not let go, to get attached emotionally, to hate to be separated (from)</li>
<li>to bite <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of hunting dogs</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вцепиться.html>вцепи́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vcepítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вцепляться.html>вцепля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vcepljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вцепиться.html>вцепи́ться</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вшивый.html>вши́вый</a> (15998)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вошь.html>вошь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vošʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вшивый.html>вши́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">všívyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)вши́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)вши́вей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lousy <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">infested with lice</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
